Japanese Celebrity Muto Assassinated

The Murderer Held a Grudge Due to Unemployment

(Tokyo) Muto Sanji (the current president of Jiji Shinpo, 67 years old this year), accompanied by two secretaries, was walking near his villa in Kamakura, Kanagawa Prefecture, at 9:10 this morning when a strange man suddenly appeared and fired a handgun, wounding Muto and killing one of the secretaries. The perpetrator then shot himself in the chest to commit suicide. Muto was shot three times and is currently being treated at Kamakura Hospital. The murdered secretary's name is Aoki Toru (23 years old). The authorities believe the perpetrator is Fukushima Shinkichi from Oku-cho, Arakawa Ward, Tokyo, and have telegraphed the Tokyo Metropolitan Police Department to investigate.

Another telegram states that Muto was severely injured in the legs, jaw, and abdomen. As a result of the authorities' investigation, the perpetrator was Fukushima Shinkichi, an unemployed person, but he has no connection with ideological groups. (Nichi Ren, 9th)

(Tokyo) Businessman Muto Sanji was shot and seriously injured by a handgun-wielding assailant at his villa in Kamakura this morning, and his life is in danger. Muto is a famous figure in Japanese financial and political circles. He served as the president of the largest cotton spinning mill, Kanebo, for 40 years. Kanebo's prosperity today is entirely due to President Muto. After resigning in 1929, he founded the Political Education Hall. He began his political movement in 1923 and was elected as a member of the Diet three times by organizing the Businessmen's Comrades Association. The Businessmen's Comrades Association was later renamed the National Comrades Association. Muto has now retired from the political world. (Nichi Ren, 9th)

Kamakura When Muto Sanji was assassinated, a police officer asked him the reason. Muto, in great pain, was unable to explain in detail, saying only, "The reason is the crematorium issue. Please ask Mr. Sakuma for details." Therefore, the Kamakura Police Station urgently summoned Muto's secretary, Mr. Sakuma, to the station. The secretary stated that the reason stemmed from a personal grudge. Fukushima planned to establish a crematorium in Kamakura last May or June and asked Muto for a donation, but Muto refused. Later, Muto announced a plan to establish a crematorium, which Fukushima was very angry about, so he decided to kill Muto to vent his anger. Fukushima also held a record of the above situation. (Nichi Ren, 9th)

Kamakura The perpetrator who attacked Muto Sanji, Fukushima Shinkichi, used to be a clerk at the Kyobashi Machinery Company. He is currently unemployed and depends on his wife, Yoshiko's, labor for a living. He decided to commit the crime and suddenly drank at home last night, then took his wife and four children to a nearby movie theater, secretly bidding farewell to his wife. As for his motive for committing the crime, after investigating his wife, it seems that there is no organization behind him. The perpetrator planned to establish a crematorium in Oku last May or June and went to see Muto to request a donation, but Muto refused and obstructed his business, so he deeply resented Muto. Recently, his life has become increasingly difficult due to unemployment, so he attacked Muto. (Dentsu, 9th)

U.S. Authorities Criticize Japan's Naval Competition

Strengthening Military Power to Maintain International Peace

Responsibility of All Countries Not to Exceed Treaty Limits

(Washington) Japanese Navy Minister Osumi's declaration that Japan will increase the construction of warships to compete with the U.S. Navy has greatly alarmed Congress and naval circles here today. In response to Osumi's remarks, Georgia Congressman Vinson (the proposer of the Vinson-Trammell Act) declared that the U.S. shipbuilding program does not exceed the scope of the naval treaty. Vinson continued, "Our shipbuilding program aims to eliminate various doubts about naval competition. Our bill aims to fulfill our responsibility for the international balance of power permitted by the treaty. Whether at home or abroad, I have not seen any reason to oppose this plan." Illinois Congressman Britten, one of the main figures advocating the large navy bill, also does not believe that the United States will engage in naval competition. Britten said, "Unless Britain and Japan automatically violate the solemn treaty concluded with us, we do not want to exceed the scope of the treaty. If any of the two countries, Britain and Japan, find our shipbuilding program objectionable, it would be clear evidence that they do not trust us." Chief of Naval Operations Admiral Standley said that the moral obligation of all countries is to maintain the full naval power permitted by the treaty. Standley continued, "All signatories to the London or Washington Treaty should preserve their full naval power to maintain a proper balance of international peace and security. The peace treaty ending the last World War failed to resolve many international difficulties after the war, especially in the Far East. The responsibility of all countries is not to exceed the limits of the treaty. I believe that maintaining the full naval power permitted by the treaty is also the obligation of all countries. If the governments of various countries allow their naval power to weaken, the international balance, peace, and security will inevitably be shaken." (National News Agency, 8th)

Comparison of U.S. and Japanese Navies

(Tokyo) The naval expansion bill proposed by U.S. Senator Vinson has been passed by both houses of Congress. When this bill is completed, that is, in 1939, the strength of the U.S. Navy will be as follows:

Battleships 15 ships 455,400 tons

Aircraft carriers 6 ships 135,000 tons

Class A cruisers 18 ships 172,650 tons

Class B cruisers 19 ships 157,600 tons

Destroyers 97 ships 150,000 tons

Submarines 40 ships 52,590 tons

Total 195 ships 1,123,240 tons

Comparing this with the strength of Japan's second replenishment plan completion period, that is, 1936, the ratio is 60% for battleships, 62% for aircraft carriers, 62% for Class A cruisers, 73% for Class B cruisers, 67% for destroyers, and 100% for submarines. Therefore, Japan will need to build more various warships after the expiration of the arms reduction treaty in 1936. (Nichi Ren, 9th)

One Cruiser, One Destroyer, Two Submarines

The Naval Committee discussed this case and has recently submitted a report advocating that the case be passed quickly, saying that the tonnage of shipbuilding this year is lower than the annual average from 1922 to 1932 and is the minimum to maintain France's naval strength. The second "Dunkerque" class armored cruiser is necessary for the even distribution of two capital ships. As for the destroyer and two submarines, they are replacing old ships that have reached the end of their service life. (Havas, 8th)

The League of Nations Holds Last Hope for Arms Reduction

Britain Agrees to Joint Sanctions Against Violations of the Convention

French Public Opinion Does Not Oppose German Rearmament

Letter from French Foreign Minister Published in Geneva

(Geneva) The League of Nations now holds a final hope for arms reduction, because Britain has changed its attitude and supports joint action against those who violate the arms reduction convention. It is also heard that influential public opinion in France has also shifted regarding the issue of German rearmament.

A white paper on the arms reduction issue was published here today, containing a letter from French Foreign Minister Barthou, explaining France's attitude in simple terms and explaining the reasons for the deadlock in negotiations, saying that France cannot accept any organization of a military nature not being regarded as an army. France also cannot agree that countries bound by military clauses of the treaty can immediately rearm, while other countries must immediately reduce armaments. The letter also stated the need for guarantees when the arms reduction convention is violated, and that some countries are actively rearming regardless of the provisions of the treaty, and this matter should be resolved quickly.

The U.S. memorandum sent to the British Ambassador on February 19 supported the British arms reduction proposal of January 29 and advocated reducing offensive armaments while increasing the defensive armaments of weak countries. The memorandum proposed: (1) Abolishing heavy artillery, large tanks, bombers, and similar weapons used for aggression; (2) Continuing automatic inspection of armaments; (3) Concluding a universal non-aggression pact. The memorandum also stated that the U.S. government will not participate in European political issues, so it will not participate in diplomatic discussions on such issues, but the U.S. government is very concerned about maintaining European peace and welcomes the efforts of the British government. The U.S. government is completely in agreement with the UK that the arms reduction convention is not only necessary but also facilitates a general easing of politics. The memorandum concluded by saying that the U.S. government hopes that the British proposal can lead to the revival of arms reduction talks. It is expected that France can reply to the British proposal of February 9 next week, and progress can be made to facilitate arms reduction negotiations. (Reuters, 9th)

French Cabinet Discusses Reply to Britain

Can Be Sent Out Next Monday

(Paris) Today it was heard that the French Foreign Ministry's reply to the British arms reduction memorandum will be issued next Monday, gently rejecting the British proposal. (National News Agency, 9th)

According to political sources, it is believed that the Foreign Minister's rescheduling of the trip is to wait for the wave of the Belgian Foreign Minister's declaration on arms reduction to pass before going to Brussels, because according to recent news from Brussels, the Belgian Foreign Minister's declaration has caused conflicts between the Belgian Nationalist Party and the Socialist Party and may involve the cabinet. In addition, the French Military Committee also met this afternoon to discuss the reply to the British arms reduction memorandum. (National News Agency, 8th)

Baldwin Says the European Situation Is Not Hopeless

Equality of Air Forces in All Countries Avoids Danger

Establishing Air Force Base in Iraq

(London) British Under-Secretary of State for Air Sassoon presented the Air Force budget in the House of Commons today, including an item of 65,000 pounds to build a new air force base in Diwaniyah, Iraq. Sassoon said that sky surveillance is very effective and described in detail the method used to quell rebellions, saying that warnings are given first, sometimes warnings are issued in the sky using loudspeakers, which is mostly effective. If it cannot be suppressed, dummy bombs are dropped as a warning. As for real bombs, they are not used lightly. Natives often gather to cause trouble, but they scatter because they see airplanes patrolling. Lord Privy Seal Baldwin, when referring to this budget, said that he could not agree with those who said that Lord President of the Council Eden's tour of Europe had failed. This trip has not yet yielded results, but he has never given up hope of establishing a convention based on the British arms reduction plan, which would allow the air forces of all countries to be equal to each other. He knows that this is a necessary condition to avoid danger. If a convention cannot be concluded, the government will not relax its efforts to seek an agreement with Western European countries to preserve European civilization. He does not acknowledge that the situation today is already hopeless, but if all efforts fail and this equality cannot be achieved, the British government will ensure that the British Air Force does not lag behind other countries. (Reuters, 8th)

Belgian Foreign Minister Reaffirms Position on Arms Reduction

Flexibility Should Be Allowed for Limiting German Armaments

There Is No Real Conflict Between the Views of France and Belgium

Brussels Foreign Minister Hymans stated in the Senate that the comments published in various newspapers mostly misunderstand the declaration on arms reduction issues made by Prime Minister de Broqueville a few days ago and his speech in the Senate. The Foreign Minister continued, "What we rely on is the common sense of the Belgian people. No one can believe that we support German rearmament. We have never said a word about this matter. Some people think that Germany must be forced to disarm in accordance with the restrictions of the Treaty of Versailles. Although this statement is reasonable, if it is for a great power, it is argued that such restrictions should be appropriately adjusted to adapt to the current situation. If we take a tough stance and do not allow flexibility, we cannot avoid being arrogant and different, and it is difficult for facts to achieve. Fortunately, France and Belgium are in complete agreement on this matter. All methods of force that are sufficient to cause war are rejected by both France and Belgium. France and Belgium both allow Germany to have troops, but they should be subject to careful restrictions and strict supervision. In addition, France and Belgium have also agreed that sanctions should be imposed if any violations of the established rules occur, and that they should act in unity at all times. This is the only way to prevent Germany's illegal rearmament." (Havas, 8th)

Brussels According to the Catholic newspaper Le Vingtième Siècle, a certain important person familiar with Belgian domestic and foreign policy made a declaration stating that Prime Minister de Broqueville publicly expressed deep doubts about the value of the military clauses in the Treaty of Versailles, believing that such clauses are insufficient to provide security, so Belgium has the right to seek other supplementary methods, such as increasing the effectiveness of the Rhineland Pact, so that the left bank of the Rhine River, as stipulated in the pact, becomes a demilitarized zone, and the security of Belgium is guaranteed by France, Britain, and Italy. It should be implemented as well, etc. (Havas, 8th)

(Paris) Foreign Minister Barthou was originally scheduled to travel to Brussels from Geneva to meet with Belgian Foreign Minister Hymans in a private capacity, but the State Council is scheduled to be held on the 12th of this month, so he could not make it in time, so the itinerary was postponed. League of Nations Suggests to All Countries the Banning of War-Mongering Broadcasts

Agreement to Manage International Radio

(Geneva) The draft international broadcasting agreement proposing international management of broadcasting to prohibit war-mongering speeches has been sent by the League of Nations Administrative Council to various countries for their consent. To make radio an effective tool for maintaining peace, this agreement will establish strict checks on radio programs, especially news and political broadcasts. All broadcasting companies should refrain from transmitting any messages that incite war sentiment or provoke international conflict. They should also ensure the accuracy of information on international relations. Governments participating in this treaty should abide by strict penalties for violating international broadcasting rules. The penalty measures are still being drafted. It has been proposed that governments should revoke the licenses or rights of broadcasting companies when broadcasting rules are systematically violated. The International Intellectual Cooperation Organization has been instrumental in the establishment of this treaty. The management of political broadcasting has long been an idea within the International Intellectual Cooperation Organization. As news from Munich indicates, Austria considers it a deliberate attempt to undermine its domestic security. The proposed international broadcasting rules are as follows: (1) Any telegram deliberately sent for a certain country, constituting a hazard to the domestic security of that country, shall be prohibited. (2) Provocative messages are not allowed to be broadcast. (3) Various messages sufficient to affect international cooperation should be prohibited. (4) Strict checks should be implemented during tense situations. (5) Incorrect messages should be corrected immediately. (6) National propaganda should include peaceful programs. These programs should include the living conditions of foreign nations, the development of mutual relations between nations, and organizations related to peace. (7) Governments should issue peaceful rules for national broadcasting. (8) If radio disputes cannot be resolved by diplomatic conventions, they should be submitted to the Hague Supreme Court or the International Intellectual Cooperation Committee. Governments may submit opinions before August 1934. The League of Nations General Assembly on September 24, 1931, resolved that the International Intellectual Cooperation Organization should investigate various international issues that arise and are sufficient to affect good international relations. The Disarmament Conference on the issue of moral disarmament was also brought to attention, believing that radio should benefit peace. (8th National Telegram)

Germany Denies Papen's Visit to Rome

This proposal not only concerns the economic cooperation of the three countries but also extends to other countries along the Danube River. London dispatch: According to reports here, Austrian Prime Minister Dollfuss and the Hungarian Prime Minister will travel to Italy together. Rome has expressed its welcome. Roman newspapers generally expect a tripartite agreement between Italy, Austria, and Hungary, and praise Mussolini's intention to consolidate the foundation of peace in the Balkans. However, Czechoslovakia and Yugoslavia have expressed alarm at the visit of the Austrian and Hungarian Prime Ministers to Italy, and expressed that they would rather see the National Socialist Party gain power in Austria. Czechoslovakia and Yugoslavia naturally oppose the alliance of countries advocating the revision of the Treaty of Trianon, as the two countries were the main beneficiaries of the treaty, while Hungary lost a significant amount of territory, and the provision that its independence should be maintained without the consent of the League of Nations. Furthermore, the alliance of Italy, Austria, and Hungary is rooted in the attempt to curb Germany's ambitions in Austria and Central Europe, so Germany also opposes it.

At the same time, Austrian Prime Minister Dollfuss is striving to realize the ideal of a Christian corporate state and celebrated the one-week anniversary of the dissolution of the Austrian Parliament yesterday (4th). In Corinthia, Dollfuss told 25,000 farmers that Austria's new constitution will be promulgated in the near future. Dollfuss also praised the workers, because Austrian workers who were loyal to the government accounted for 90% during the recent Social Democratic uprising. Dollfuss also stated that Austria is prepared to establish reciprocal tariffs with Hungary, but without establishing a customs union. We have obtained the foundation of Austria's welfare. Austria is now able to be self-reliant and does not need to rely on others.

Here and in various cities in Europe, there is much speculation about whether Dollfuss can overcome his key subordinates, such as Deputy Prime Minister Emil Fey and Internal Guard Commander Prince Starhemberg. It is known that Dollfuss opposes severely punishing Social Democratic members arrested in recent disturbances, while Fey and Prince Starhemberg advocate severe punishment. The Austrian Social Democratic Party anticipates a large increase in National Socialist Party members. However, many Austrian workers fear the retaliatory actions of the National Socialist Party. The Austrian and Hungarian Prime Ministers will arrive in Rome around March 12. The main purpose of the Austrian and Hungarian Prime Ministers' visit to Italy has been officially announced, which is to discuss with Mussolini the plan for the economic methods of the Danube River countries proposed by Mussolini. However, as a result of the consultation between the three Prime Ministers of Italy, Austria, and Hungary, Italy may be able to support the restoration of the Austro-Hungarian Empire. This step will inevitably be opposed, because the restoration of the Austro-Hungarian Empire must be accompanied by the requirement to build defensive fortifications on the Austro-Hungarian border. (Foreign Press)

US Congress Supports Roosevelt

Grants Power to Increase or Decrease Tariffs

(Washington) President Roosevelt and Democratic leaders met at the White House today. The leaders promised to find ways to pass the various bills that have been submitted and not resolved before Congress adjourns in mid-May, especially focusing on the tariff plan, which will allow the President to increase or decrease tariffs, as a preliminary step in considering the war debt problem. Senator Robinson said today that President Roosevelt's war debt message to Congress will be purely informative in nature and will not require legislative procedures. The issue of the United States joining the International Court of Justice will be shelved indefinitely. (9th Reuters Telegram)

(Washington) Secretary of State Hull presented a draft law to the House Ways and Means Committee, requesting that President Roosevelt be granted full power to amend tariffs. In his speech, Hull said that this draft law is extremely important, because if we want to restore international trade and make it practically possible, the only feasible policy is to conclude commercial treaties separately with various countries. Trade wars benefit no one. Various restrictions on international trade are bound to cause serious disputes and even provoke wars. As a result of international trade wars, when goods cannot circulate, phenomena such as overproduction, unemployment, and capital outflow are bound to follow. Conversely, if international trade can develop according to normal conditions, the total amount of international trade in the world can be increased from the current 1.3 million US dollars to 5 million US dollars. The purpose of the bill recently submitted by the government to the House is to restore trade relations between countries, so that our country and other countries can benefit from it. We deeply hope to reopen the old markets that have been closed and at the same time find new markets for selling goods. As for the most-favored-nation treatment clause, it will still be maintained. In conclusion, Hull said that the bill proposed by the government is based on the common benefit of all countries to restore international trade, so this bill is not only sufficient to assist the economic recovery of the world, but also a powerful element of peace and culture. (Harriman Havas Telegram)

That is, its organization, in addition to the top management, should organize a deliberative council to assist the top management. Minister of Colonial Affairs Nagai expressed his support for this, saying that Yu agrees with Okura. The South Manchurian Railway is a special company with the mission of special national policy. It is not the time to change the South Manchurian Railway into a state-owned company today. Yu's intention is to still cooperate with the South Manchurian Railway today. After answering the questions of Sakamoto Toshiatsu, the minister of finance, on the fuel national policy issue, the meeting adjourned at 4:00 pm. The budget will be approved at the General Budget Assembly on the 9th, and it can be passed without incident. (9th Electrical Communication Telegram)

Resolutions of the Anti-Opium Association

(Nanjing) The Anti-Opium Committee held its 131st meeting on the 9th. Liu Ruiheng and others attended. Resolutions: (1) Regarding the draft of the International Convention for the Suppression of Illicit Traffic in Narcotic Drugs, after detailed study, it was generally agreed that our country is a victim of narcotic drugs, and the aforementioned Convention for the Suppression of Illicit Traffic is beneficial to our country. It was resolved to express support and to inform the Ministry of Foreign Affairs accordingly. (2) A type of native product called "Tu Ma" produced in Xinjiang Province was sent to the National Health Administration for chemical testing. The results proved that it is similar to Indian hemp, and its narcotic effect is stronger than that of Indian hemp. It was resolved to inform the Xinjiang Provincial Government to strictly prohibit it in accordance with the provisions of the Anti-Opium Law, and to notify all provincial and municipal governments to prohibit it uniformly. International Commercial Telegram

丨Reuter's Exclusive Commercial Telegram, March 9丨

Gold and Silver: London Gold Price - Today's London gold price is 136 shillings and 10 pence, up 2 pence from yesterday.

London Bullion: Today's London silver price is 20 pence 25 for spot and 20 pence 375 for futures, both down 1875, because there are no buyers and China has sold a little. Speculators bought when prices fell, and the market closed steadily.

New York Silver Price: Today's silver market is firm and bullish. The fall in London silver prices started with selling pressure. The price difference in the American market was thus restored. The market here was quite active in the morning, and the price rose 50 points, exceeding the London parity price. Later, due to profit-taking, the upward momentum was stopped. Therefore, the futures opened, with the May contract down 25 points, and the rest up 4 to 20 points from yesterday's close.

Bombay Silver Price: Today's Bombay silver market closed steadily. The spot price is 55 rupees and 15 annas, up 6 annas.

Exchange Rates

British-American Exchange Rates: The London foreign exchange market fluctuated very little, with only slight fluctuations. The British-American exchange rate opened at $5.0775, the same as yesterday's closing price for the US-British exchange rate. The Current State of the European Gold Standard (London Correspondence)

The Gold Standard Inevitably Shakes

France Makes Every Effort to Maintain It

Before the World Economic Conference last year, we all knew that the tune of so-called international cooperation was sung very high, and many people had great hopes for it, thinking that even if the whole problem could not be solved, at least a superficial conclusion could be reached on the technical aspects. Unexpectedly, at the very beginning, a major upheaval occurred regarding international currency stabilization, and international cooperation was thus declared a failure, and international disputes were intensified. Britain had already abandoned the gold standard, and needless to say, the United States was also preparing to use an inflationary policy to subdue its domestic panic. Thereupon, the European countries that had suffered from inflated currencies began to unite. The countries participating in this alliance at that time were France, Italy, Belgium, the Netherlands, Switzerland, and Poland, with the common goal of defending the gold standard to the death, forming a European economic alliance centered on France.

Now the United States has formally announced a reduction in the pure gold content of the US dollar, and the problem can be said to be very serious. The future of the gold standard can also be said to be very critical. However, it is a question worth our attention as to how things will change in the future. Judging from the current situation, they probably will not abandon the gold standard in the short term. The reasons are as follows:

(1) The four economically strong countries of France, Belgium, the Netherlands, and Switzerland still maintain huge amounts of cash. France has 80 billion francs, Belgium has 2.7 billion Belgas, the Netherlands has 768 million florins, and Switzerland has almost 800 million francs. Moreover, their foreign short-term investments are very small, so the flight of domestic capital abroad is not very intense. Therefore, they still have the strength to maintain the gold standard.

(2) Among the six countries in the gold standard alliance, four have deeply felt the pain of currency inflation. Their people strongly oppose the paper money policy. If the gold standard is stopped, the currency inflation policy will naturally follow. Then political struggles will become more intense, and riots are feared to occur. Strikes and other actions that disrupt social order cannot be ruled out. These are all experiences that the German and French countries have had in the past, and they are certainly unwilling to take risks again.

(3) The countries in continental Europe that have implemented currency inflation policies have not stabilized their currencies for many years, and it has not been long since they regained the credibility lost by the inflation policy. If the gold standard is stopped, they will lose credibility again. Therefore, they now want to fix the credibility of the gold standard, and conversely, they oppose adopting the suspension of the gold standard.

However, France has a major contradiction: First, the outflow of cash cannot be underestimated. Second, last year's visible trade deficit was nearly 1 billion francs. Third, foreign investment is gradually being recovered, and interest income will naturally decrease. Therefore, since last year, more than 6 billion francs have fled abroad. This number is indeed not to be easily overlooked. Moreover, France has worked hard to prevent the hiding of cash and increase income from ships and the like, but the world economy has not really improved, so France will certainly not be able to avoid its adverse effects. Therefore, maintaining the gold standard is not easy. On the other hand, the cash reserve ratio of the franc is still 92%, and the general middle class supports the gold standard, and the political tendency is towards a strong cabinet, then the gold standard seems to be able to continue for some time.

The Netherlands is considered a relatively strong country in Europe, but since last year, the import and export trade, compared with 1929, has fallen by almost one-third. In the early spring of last year, prices fell, and by winter, they were forced to increase by 5% by artificial methods, but there was no substantive improvement. The source of her livelihood is the market of the Dutch East Indies. In 1929, she ranked first in imports to the area, but by last year, this market was seized by Japanese goods. Japanese goods imported into the Dutch East Indies accounted for 56% of the total imports, squeezing the Netherlands to second place. As a result, unemployment continues to increase in the country, and both the textile industry and the coal mines are panicking. Recently, there have been proposals to ally with Britain to resist Japanese goods.

Belgium is considered a country that can maintain fiscal balance. Its cash reserve can also maintain a level of more than 2.6 billion Belgas, which is a country that supports the gold standard. Besides France, Belgium is the one that matters.

Switzerland is the weakest link in the gold standard countries. First, there are financial difficulties. Last year, the income was insufficient by about 100 million francs. The difficulties in foreign trade are also because the watches manufactured in the country are not easy to sell, so export trade is always declining. In fact, what Switzerland relies on is the income from foreign tourists. First, because Swiss prices are higher than in any European country, and second, because the economic situation is not good, there are few tourists. The closure of Swiss hotels is now even affecting the financial turnover of banks.

Germany in the European gold standard countries is already in a precarious situation, and Italy is also difficult to sustain. Relying on France alone will not work. Economic insecurity will easily affect politics in the future. (February 2, 1934, London)

Research on the Future of the Saito Cabinet (Japanese Correspondence)

Partition by Various Parties

Speculation on Successors

The evolution of the Japanese political situation, since Mr. Okamoto's blatant questioning, has caused a huge political uproar. Although Mr. Okamoto's investigation of the Eisaku Sato bribery case has come to an end, the Saito Cabinet is not stable because of this. On the contrary, the movement of party splits has become more obvious. Hatoyama has now resigned, and the position of Minister of Education is temporarily held by Saito concurrently. The Saito Cabinet has not collapsed, but the attackers are still proceeding, and the issue of Railway Minister Mitsuchi is about to rise again, so the matter of the Saito Cabinet's resignation en masse is still being actively brewed. It probably is not without meaning to talk about the succeeding cabinet now.

After the Saito Cabinet, some say that Saito will be reappointed to form a cabinet, some say that the current Governor-General of Korea, Ugaki Kazushige, will succeed, some say that Hiranuma Kiichirō will form a cabinet, and there are also Takahashi Korekiyo, Konoe Fumimaro, and Ichiki Kitokurō who may be appointed to form a cabinet.

The reason why Saito Makoto has been able to maintain it until now is that he is a veteran of the navy and has a good reputation among the military. Secondly, he is very generous and can indeed accommodate and reconcile between the army and the navy. He also does not excessively destroy constitutional politics and still maintains the face of parliamentary politics. He is also not very harsh on capitalists. Therefore, in the turbulent political tide, he can always manage to get through it.

The most promising candidate is Ugaki Kazushige. He is the first person after Tanaka Giichi among the elders of the Japanese military. He has almost formed the Okayama faction himself, and most of the general class support him. He also has a good relationship with the Minseitō party, and the deputies under the Minseitō are also willing to support him. However, the staff officer class under the military丨丨i.e., colonels, lieutenant colonels, and majors, which the Japanese call the core class丨丨are very dissatisfied with him. The reason for their dissatisfaction is that first, Ugaki is close to the political parties and does not follow the ways of the military clique. Second, Ugaki advocates preserving parliamentary politics, which is very inconvenient for the military dictatorship movement. Therefore, the core class would rather support Araki or Masaki than Ugaki. Then, even if the Minseitō party enthusiastically supports him, the result will still be unable to take the stage, because the real power of the Japanese military is almost in the hands of the core class. If the core class opposes it, there will inevitably be more difficulties in politics. It is now unknown whether the people in the core class can change their attitude.

The next most promising figure is Hiranuma Kiichirō, who is known to the world. The center of the Hiranuma cabinet-formation movement is the Kokuhonsha and various right-wing groups related to the Kokuhonsha. Hayashi Senjūrō in the army and Katō Kanji in the navy have both expressed their goodwill towards him. The Satsuma faction in Kazuyama Sukehide (member of the House of Peers) also emphasized advocating the so-called Hiranumaism to help Hiranuma, but Hiranumaism has been advocated for so long, but it still cannot take the stage. The reason is that his relationship with the elder statesmen is not good, especially those who advocate the theory of constitutional common sense, such as Kinmochi Saionji, are even worse towards him, but Interior Minister Nobuaki Makino has a fairly good feeling towards Hiranuma. Among the people in the House of Representatives, some members of the Kokumin Domei led by Nakanō Seigō are also expressing goodwill towards Hiranuma, and even some members of the Tokuji faction are willing to support Hiranuma. After the internal strife in the Seiyūkai party this time, the Kūhara Fusanosuke stream also communicated with Hiranuma, so the optimistic theory of Hiranuma's cabinet formation has gradually risen again recently.

Again, the most popular and politically skilled among the nobles is Konoe Fumimaro. According to the current situation, if Konoe organizes a transcendent cabinet, there will be no problems in both houses. However, the elder statesmen believe that Konoe is indeed talented and can be greatly used, but in the current chaotic situation, it seems unnecessary to sacrifice him, so the feasibility of Konoe's cabinet is not very high now.

Ichiki Kitokurō is also a suitable prime minister in the Japanese political world, but because of the London Treaty issue, his opinions with the military have not yet been satisfactory. At this time, the military supports everything, and it is therefore even more difficult for Ichiki to form a cabinet.

As for the Kiyoura Keigo Cabinet, it is essentially very similar to Saito. It is even less the time for Araki to form a cabinet now. It is even less likely that Suzuki Saburō, Wakatsuki Reijirō, and others will take the stage as party leaders. (March 1, 1934, Tokyo)

Sun Dianying's Troops are Reorganized by Jin Fang

Fu Zhan Kui Agrees to Meet Sun at Dengkou

Lu Fengnian Suggests Sun's Troops Surrender to Jin Fang

Beijing Correspondence: The Sun Dianying incident, as of now, is still being resolved more by military means. Fu Zhan Kui is currently staying at Huangyangmutou and has telegraphed Sun Dianying, agreeing to meet Sun at Dengkou, but Sun has not replied. Because there is news that the Jin army is advancing toward Dengkou in the near future. As for Lu Fengnian of Sun's troops in Dengkou, he sent a representative, Yu Muxing, to Beijing the other day to meet with He Yingqin, expressing that he could urge Sun to leave the army, but hoped that his troops would be reorganized by Jin Fang. This morning (8th), according to the spokesman of the Military Sub-Committee, the authorities' method for Sun's troops has always remained unchanged from the original proposal. If Sun Dianying can be made to leave the army, Sun's troops will be withdrawn to their original defense, and downsized according to the number on file in accordance with the order of the Military Sub-Committee, then it is not impossible for Jin Fang to reorganize the troops. It is reported that Yu Muxing will stay in Beijing for about three days before leaving Beijing.

Since Fu Zuoyi returned to Suiyuan, the military operations have become more urgent. The rear troops left in Suiyuan have all moved westward, with the majority of troops advancing towards Dengkou, and before Fu Zhan Kui and Sun Dianying's negotiations have yielded results, Sun's troops will be subjected to the greatest threat, in order to make the troops submit. All personnel of Fu Zuoyi's military headquarters have arrived in Baotou. After the eastern Suiyuan troops moved westward, the defense was filled in by the Zhou Yuanjian Brigade of Li Fuying's troops. As for the Xu Zizhen Regiment of the 70th Division of the Wang Jingguo troops, which was responsible for the vanguard, it did have contact with more than 1,000 cavalrymen of the Peng Zhen Brigade of Sun's army. The Peng Brigade could not support it and retreated westward. The Xu Regiment then occupied the area. This was the first conflict between the Jin Sui army and Sun's troops. After the Xu Regiment made some adjustments, it also cooperated with the cavalry of Zhao Chengshou's troops and the 205th and 215th Brigades to actively advance westward according to the original plan. When they arrived near the Huangtulahai River, they found more than 1,000 of Sun's troops resisting and defending. After the Jin Sui army once carried out a fierce artillery bombardment, Sun's troops were again unable to support it and fled in the southwest direction. The Jin Sui army tracked and chased fiercely. This was the second conflict. The vanguard of the current Jin Sui army has been forced to Dengkou, confronting the Lu Fengnian troops of Sun's 119th Division. If Sun's meeting with Fu Zhan Kui still yields no results, the Jin Sui army will attack Dengkou. It is reported that Sun himself has expressed to people that he is willing to leave the army and downsize his troops in accordance with the order, but he still strongly advocates the realization of the matter of the troops going to Qinghai to cultivate wasteland, so that they can have a way out. Sun's division commander, Lu Fengnian, has suggested to Sun that Sun's entire jurisdiction should be handed over to Jin Fang for reorganization, so as to avoid scattering. Sun also expressed sympathy for this. When Sun leaves the army in the future, he may hand over the entire command to Lu for reorganization and surrender to Jin Fang. Moreover, Lu Fengnian and Sun are from the same hometown. More than ten years ago, he served as a division commander in the Jin army. Last year, he was appointed by Sun as the division commander of the 119th Division of the army and also has a good feeling for Jin Fang.

A certain member of the Military Sub-Committee in Beijing talked about how Fu Zhankui, who went to Dengkou to meet Sun Zhanying, had arrived at Huangyangmutou and was heading towards Dengkou. Sun Zhanying was indeed in the Mandahai area near Ningyuan, but Sun had ordered his troops to inform Li Ming, the staff officer of the Military Sub-Committee who arrived in Dengkou, that he would return to Dengkou to meet Fu. Regardless of whether Sun accepts the advice to leave the army, it is expected that if the two men of Fu and Sun can meet, there will be progress. The military authorities, because Sun's attitude is uncertain and there is no considerable certainty of a peaceful solution, have always actively carried out military preparations. The war situation in the Ningyuan area is not as serious as rumored. There have only been small contacts between the two sides. The Military Sub-Committee has already decided on the steps for the Sun issue yesterday, but it depends on how the results of Fu Zhankui's meeting with Sun are before implementing the established plan. (8th)

The Reason for Du Qiyun's Execution in Beijing

The Crime of Colluding with Ronin

Conspiring to Overthrow the Government

Xiamen Correspondence: When the Central Army entered Fujian to suppress the rebellion, Du Qiyun was ordered to be the Fujian Military Commissioner. After the military ended, Du flew from Xiamen to the provincial capital on February 1. On the same day, he was detained by Provincial Chairman Chen Yi upon receiving a telegram order from Chairman Chiang Kai-shek. On the 8th, Chiang sent someone from Fujian to escort him to Nanjing. After that, the news was silent. Recently, it has been widely rumored in Xiamen that he was executed in Beijing. Du's relatives and friends in Xiamen telegraphed Beijing to inquire about Du's relatives, and received a reply stating that "Du died of a sudden illness." Therefore, Du's death was confirmed. Yesterday, political circles here received the news that Du was shot on February 28. The so-called sudden death from a sudden illness was actually execution. His crimes were "colluding with ronin, organizing institutions, and conspiring to overthrow the government." It turns out that after Du recovered Xiamen, he set up a military commissioner's office in Xiamen. During this period, Du actually colluded with ronin from a certain side to organize the South China State. More than 40 people had already signed the petition, and Du was elected as the leader. Someone reported the incident to Chiang Kai-shek, and a certain side searched for important documents, including the signing register at the time, and submitted them to Beijing. Chiang Kai-shek immediately ordered Du to be detained and escorted to Beijing for questioning. In addition to the strong physical evidence, there were also important personnel from Fujian who went to Beijing to testify. Therefore, Du was sentenced to death. Due to certain relations, it was announced to the outside world that he died suddenly. According to Du, whose name is Jinzhai, he is from Hubei. He served as a soldier in western Fujian for many years. He was first the subordinate of Wang Xianchen, and then rose to the brigade commander of the 3rd Division of Li Fengxiang. In 15 years of the Republic of China, during the battle of the Party Army entering Fujian, Du led his brigade and Cao Wanshun's brigade to revolt, causing Zhou Yinren's elite troops to be completely lost. The Party Army was able to recover Xiamen, and it was not without slight effort. Unexpectedly, he died of colluding with ronin, organizing institutions, and conspiring to overthrow the government. (March 7)

Special Taxes are Opened in Fujian Province

Tax Revenues are Used to Fund Bandit Suppression and Revitalize the Countryside

Fuzhou Correspondence: Regarding the opening of special taxes in this province, the authorities have been planning for a long time, and it was only recently established. The name is the驻闽办事处 (Zhu Min Ban Shi Chu) Fujian Office, with the head of the office being She Tian, and the deputy head being Gao Guangqian. The office is located in Yijiangfan, Fuzhou. Its implementation plan starts with Fuzhou and Xiamen. Fuzhou will be handled by the office itself, and a separate sub-office will be set up in Xiamen, with Yang Tianyu as the head and Chen Desen as the deputy head. They are scheduled to take the boat to Xiamen on the 8th and start working on the 10th. As for its method, it is planned to start with investigating accumulated special goods. The following are the five articles of the brief chapter that were promulgated yesterday: (1) Merchants in various counties who have accumulated unsold special goods, regardless of the quantity, shall report the types, quantities, and quantities of the inventory to the office for verification and registration within ten days from the date of the announcement of the verification. (2) After the office reports the quantity of unsold goods, it will send personnel to investigate and affix labels. (3) If the report is not made within the deadline, or if the report is made with more reports and less reports, once it is found out, in addition to confiscating the goods, all those who conceal and sell the goods will be severely punished according to military law. (4) In the future, special goods that must be affixed with verification labels will be allowed to be sold. (5) This brief chapter will be announced and implemented from the date of approval by the Provincial Government. It is heard that the special goods accumulated in this province can be sold for at least three years, so it does not interfere with the policy of prohibiting the planting of opium seedlings. As for the tax revenue, half of it is used to fund the bandit suppression, so as to quell the Red Disaster, and half is used to run the Farmers' Bank, so as to seek to revitalize the countryside. It is different from the previous forced planting of opium seedlings and forced collection of donations. However, the people who operate this special goods business in Fuzhou and Xiamen are all Taiwanese citizens and are not subject to Chinese law. Government offices have never had the right to intervene. If taxes are suddenly levied on these people without contact, conflicts will inevitably arise. During the era of the pseudo-People's Government, the guards of the Smoking Ban Supervision Office were killed on the street due to conflicts with Taiwanese people. After the incident, there was no way to negotiate. Therefore, the Special Tax Office is now in contact with Taiwanese people, allowing Taiwanese people to open foreign firms in Fuzhou and Xiamen to sell special goods, but they must pay taxes and affix certificates upon import in accordance with the regulations. (March 7)

Tragic Shipwreck in Yue River

Electric Boat Overturns in Sihui

More Than Two Hundred Passengers Killed

Guangzhou Correspondence: In the Zhujiang River basin of Guangdong Province, there are many ports and forks, and transportation in all counties is by waterway. Therefore, the embankments and river crossings in the provincial capital are crowded. In the past, ferries in various villages mostly used small steamships for transportation. Recently, they have mostly switched to electric boats, because electric boats are twice as fast as ferries. The electric boats are constructed with a flat bottom and shallow draft. Although they travel fast, they are not as safe as ferries. Recently, the newly installed electric boat Sihai, which runs between Guangzhou and Sihui County, has a very prosperous business. Passengers benefit from its fast round trip and are happy to take it. On the morning of the 4th of this month, the Sihai electric boat carried 450 passengers from Sihui County to the province. After the ship had been traveling for more than ten hours, at about 5:00 in the evening, when it sailed to the river surface of the Shitou Da Chongkou in the south of the province, just as it was about to reach Guangzhou, the bottom of the boat suddenly hit a reef and pierced a hole. River water poured in, and the people on the boat screamed for help and squeezed each other. The ship tilted, and after a while, it overturned. The cries shook the sky. Only those who knew how to swim escaped for their lives. The rest were drowned. The boatmen nearby heard the warning and rushed to rescue them in their boats. The patrol boat of the South Shitou Water Police Station, the water rescue team, and the civilian boats of the Fangbian Hospital also arrived after hearing the news to try to rescue them. More than 60 passengers drifting on the river surface were rescued, and another 20 were rescued in various ways. A total of 80 or 90 people were rescued. At the same time, more than 90 bodies were recovered. The rescue team of Fangbian Hospital also recovered four batches of bodies, the first batch of 45 male bodies and 12 female bodies, the second batch of 52 male and female bodies, the third batch of 57 bodies, and the fourth batch of more than 20 bodies. As of the afternoon of the 5th, the search was still in progress. It is estimated that 167 male and female passengers have been drowned. The remaining number of those trapped in the boat has not yet been determined. The bodies were transported to the former Yigang of Fangbian Hospital by freight car for numbering and photographing to await identification by the relatives of the deceased. Only more than 30 of them are known by name. The rest are unknown and have no relatives to claim them. The bodies will be coffined and buried in the Wuzhagang Cemetery of Yidi by the Fangbian Hospital at 2 pm on the 6th. As for the more than 80 survivors who were rescued, most of them have returned home by themselves or sought refuge with relatives. Among them, there are still 14 people who have no relatives to rely on in the province and are temporarily taken in by Fangbian Hospital to provide assistance for their return to Sihui and Guangning, their places of origin. It was also found that the 32 sailors of the electric boat were fortunate enough to swim and escape. As for the seven or eight accountants and staff members on the boat, they have all been drowned. (March 6)

Anhui's People's Wealth and Two Offices Rectify Autumn Grain Collection

Draft Measures for Various Counties to Investigate and Report Disasters

Anqing Correspondence: In Anhui Province, the handling of autumn grain collection in previous years has been fraught with abuses. Among the 61 counties in the province, only 14 counties, including Lian County, Xiuning, Wuyuan, Qimen, Yi County, Jixi, Jing County, Ningguo, Jingde, Taiping, Shidai, Guangde, Liu'an and Shan, have never handled disasters. And 9 counties, including Xuancheng, Nanling, Wuhu, Langxi, Shucheng, Mengcheng, Taihe, Woyang, and Chu County, do not request investigation even if they have not actually suffered a disaster. All land taxes are collected in full according to the amount. More than 30 counties, including Huaining, report disasters and request investigation whenever there is occasional maladjustment of rain and sunshine. This long-standing habit is unbreakable. In previous autumn grain collections, the determination of the number of mature collections must be repeatedly ordered to be rejected and returned several times before a decision can be made. As a result, the reduction or delay of the annual land tax to be collected is more than 600,000 yuan. In years with serious disasters, it is more than this. This reduction or delay of land tax in counties that break the string to offset collection (such as Huaining, Taihu, Guichi, and Zhizhi counties, there is no such corruption), the rest mostly do not distinguish between disasters and maturity, and collect in general. For example, if the tax amount is 100,000 yuan, and the autumn harvest is determined to be 80%, officials are also collected. For flower households, regardless of whether they have been affected by the disaster or not, they are still collected according to 100%. After collecting 80,000 yuan, the rest is treated as a disaster relief and stopped. As a result, the real disaster households still pay 100% of the grain silver, and cunning people delay and resist payment, waiting to escape. And the abuses such as clerks selling disasters and reducing discounts for private collection also arise because of this. Recently, the two offices of the People's Livelihood and Finance have specially drafted measures for various counties to investigate and report disasters based on the regulations on investigating and reporting disasters promulgated by the Central Government, and submitted them to the recent provincial government standing committee for approval. The original text is as follows: Article 1. When there are disasters such as floods, droughts, typhoons, hailstorms, and insect damage in various counties of this province, in addition to the regulations on investigating and reporting disasters, the provisions of this method shall be followed. Article 2. When disasters occur in various places, such as drought and insect disasters, the county magistrate shall personally visit the site for investigation and immediately report it to the Department of Civil Affairs and the Department of Finance within 10 days. In the case of typhoons, hailstorms, floods, and other urgent disasters, the report shall be made within 3 days. The committee members will be sent to the county for re-investigation and reported for approval. The deadline for summer disasters is the day before the beginning of autumn, and the deadline for autumn disasters is the day before the beginning of the science. Those who report after the deadline will not be investigated. Article 3. After the county magistrate and the committee members have re-investigated, they shall calculate the number of land taxes that should be exempted or delayed according to the severity of the disaster and the limits of exemption and delay stipulated in the regulations on investigating and reporting disasters. They shall prepare a list of districts, villages, land areas, household names, and tax numbers, draw a picture, affix a statement, and add a conclusion, and submit it separately for approval. Article 4. If the land tax to be paid in the disaster area is not exempted or delayed in full, the number of percent actually collected shall be added to the grain string according to the number of percent determined by the investigation, and the number of percent of exemption or delay shall be marked, and collected by percentage. Article 5. The land tax for land without disasters shall still be collected in full according to the amount, and shall not be combined with the disaster land to reduce the percentage. Article 6. If the people report the disaster falsely, they shall be investigated and dealt with after the county finds out the truth. The county magistrate who fabricates the disaster situation and accepts illicit regulations shall be dismissed from office and punished. Article 7. The committee members shall personally visit the disaster area to investigate each mu of land for investigation. If they support the fabrication of reports and accept illicit regulations, they shall be severely punished according to law. Article 8. After this method is promulgated, the evil habit of collecting in general without distinguishing between disasters and maturity shall be eliminated. If there are unscrupulous officials, gentry, or scholars who hold back and obstruct, they shall be dismissed, punished, or arrested separately. Article 9. If there are any matters not covered by this method, they may be submitted for amendment at any time. Article 10. This method shall be promulgated and implemented after being resolved by the provincial government meeting. (March 7)

Execution by Firing Squad of Gu Zixiang, Notorious Bandit of Nanhui

Gu Zixiang, a ringleader of bandits from Datuan, together with his gang, armed and robbed two families, Tan Pingqi and Tan Houxiang, in Pengshou Township, District 9, in April of the year before last. He also shot and wounded the victims. After the county government apprehended the culprit, he was repeatedly interrogated, and his confessions were found to be conclusive. He was sentenced to death and the sentence was approved by the provincial government. Yesterday at 4 PM, he was brought to the court for identification. After confirming his identity, he was escorted to the execution grounds outside Nanmen (South Gate) and executed by firing squad. It is said that the culprit had many accomplices. Recently, Lin Zhengfeng and others, who were arrested and sent to the province for falsely reporting the discovery of a large quantity of military supplies on the coast, were close friends of the culprit. The previous time Lin and others accompanied Xi Zhonghong, the chief of the first section of the fourth division of the provincial government, to Nanhui to investigate the case, they visited the prison to see Gu Zixiang, intending to find a way to rescue him. Fortunately, County Magistrate Yuan discovered this early and did not fall for Lin's treacherous scheme.

Suzhou Residents Tao Boye and Others Initiate a Factory to Manufacture Cigarette Rolling Paper

In recent years, observing the vast and increasing financial drain caused by cigarette smoking in society, Chinese people have started setting up factories to manufacture cigarettes themselves. However, the rolling paper used for cigarettes is still imported. Therefore, Suzhou residents Tao Boye and others have initiated a factory to manufacture it themselves by raising funds. The planned capital is one million yuan. After repeated meetings and discussions, progress has been made recently. In addition to many participants from Fujian, many Shanghai cigarette factories have also joined as shareholders. The factory site is located near Fengqiao in Suzhou, because the water there is very clear and has been tested to produce good, clean, and white paper. When the factory opens, the number of workers will be at least 300, half men and half women.

Luguang Township Robbery Case

More than ten bandits broke into the house of Sheng Zenghu, a resident of Huajiaqiao Township, Luguang, the night before last, and committed robbery. Sheng woke up from his dream and immediately fled. The bandits spotted him, chased him, and shot him in the head when they could not catch him. Then, they captured him, beat him with ropes, and burned him all over with fire. Subsequently, they robbed him of clothing, silver dollars, and other items, worth about one hundred yuan.

Songjiang Second District Boy Scout Leadership Conference

The Jiangsu Province Second District Boy Scout Leadership Conference, including leaders from twelve counties such as Songjiang, Shanghai, Nanhui, Fengxian, Chuansha, Baoshan, Qingpu, Jinshan, Jiading, Taicang, Chongming, Qidong, Haimen, and Nantong Rugao, is being held in the auditorium of the Songjiang County Party Headquarters for two days starting today (the 9th). Alarming Rumors About Power Outage

The Shanghai Electric Company suddenly announced today that due to damage to the small chimney in the boiler, power supply would be suspended for seven days starting today. Upon receiving the news, citizens were alarmed. Since the power was normally cut off last night, how could they know in advance that the small chimney was damaged? And why were both the large and small machines damaged at the same time? Why would repairs take as long as seven days? People were shocked and suspicious. Li Zuhua, the district head of the First District, was also deeply dissatisfied because the current winter defense had not yet ended, and local security was related to bandits. Without prior approval from the competent authorities, they rashly cut off the power. Moreover, it was during a dark night. In addition to sending an assistant to inspect the company and sending a letter warning them to shorten the repair time, he also informed the public security authorities that during the power outage, special attention must be paid to local security. The County Chamber of Commerce also sent a letter to the company, urging them to complete the repairs and restore power as soon as possible to maintain security. It is unknown how the company will handle this. Local people are saying that the power outage was announced when the new and old managers of the company were in dispute, with some suspecting that it was a prearranged step. Whether this is true remains to be verified.

A Baffling Swindle in Wuxi

On the morning of the 3rd, a man named Rong Zhongjing from Shanghai arrived at the Huashang Hotel on Tongyun Road outside Guangfu Gate. He was dressed in a Western suit and claimed to be the director of the Beijing engineering project for the Xin Cheng Ji Construction Company in Shanghai. He said that he had come to Wuxi under the commission of the main factory to contract for the rice flour company and also produce pickles, with a capital of 1.5 million yuan. The site had already been surveyed at Jie Jingqiao, outside Nanmen, and the construction cost was estimated at 150,000 yuan. After booking Room 22 at the hotel, he went around contacting various businesses. Later, Zhang Juexian, the owner of the Gongda Brick Factory on Jiaoji Road, and Gong Yaomao, the owner of the Shunxiangxing Sheet Metal Shop, learned about it and went to contact him for business. Rong claimed to Zhang and Gong that the company would need a total of 2.2 million bricks and 7,000 to 8,000 yuan worth of sheet metal, and asked if they could sell them at wholesale prices. Zhang and Gong were overjoyed at the prospect of such a large business and invited him to Taiheyuan for a banquet to promote business. The next day, Rong also went to the Taisan brand cement company on Liangxi Road to contact manager Sun Baoshun, and told the company's director Yang Zhongzi that he was currently applying for a construction permit from the Wuxi County Construction Bureau, which required 150 yuan, and he was short a few dozen yuan. Yang, also for business reasons, lent him 20 yuan. Afterwards, Rong contacted several bamboo shops such as Yu Yongfeng Bamboo Shop in Zhuchang Lane. However, yesterday Rong suddenly disappeared without saying goodbye, and his whereabouts were unknown. The various shops then realized that they had been swindled and are now searching for him to negotiate.

Dispute Over Bean Transactions Resolved

The Bengbu Grain Transportation and other public associations, opposing the change in bean transactions between Wuxi and Liang Counties, sent representatives led by Li Peisheng to Wuxi for negotiations. The details of the situation have been reported in this newspaper. At 3 PM on the 8th, the County Chamber of Commerce specially convened relevant parties from the three counties of Bengbu, Wuxi, and Liang to attempt mediation. More than twenty people including Sun Yuanfu attended. Qian Sunqing, a standing committee member of the Wuxi Chamber of Commerce, served as the temporary chairman. First, representatives from both sides expressed their opinions, with each side sticking to their own arguments. Subsequently, through the efforts of Qian Sunqing and Chen Zhanru of the Wuxi Chamber of Commerce, and Lin Junbao of the Wujin Chamber of Commerce, a resolution was finally reached. The agreed-upon principles of mediation are as follows: For soybean transactions in Wuxi and Liang, the Bengbu commission deduction method should be followed. If the price rises above five yuan, a 99% exchange rate should be used. However, since the current market price is below five yuan, the established 98.4% exchange rate in Wuxi and Liang should be revised to 96% to respect the wishes of the Bengbu merchants, limited to the north-south river beans of Bengbu, and implemented from the 10th of this month, in order to maintain mutual interests and ensure the stability of each business. After these principles were decided, representatives from the three counties of Bengbu, Wuxi, and Liang unanimously agreed and signed the original text of the principles. The meeting adjourned at around 9 PM. The three Bengbu representatives then hosted a banquet at the New World Western Restaurant for the committee members of the Wuxi and Wujin Chambers of Commerce, representatives of the rice and bean industry, and reporters from local newspapers. The guests and hosts mingled and celebrated until 11 PM before dispersing. It is also heard that the three Bengbu representatives and the Wujin representative left Wuxi yesterday to return to Bengbu.

Government Car Derails While Turning

In order to improve railway operations and ensure passenger safety, the Beijing-Shanghai Railway Bureau specially dispatched the chief engineer, a foreigner named Bai Huaide, to inspect the route. Bai arrived in Wuxi on the 8th on the 12:00 express train from Shanghai to Beijing, staying in Government Car No. 3. Yesterday morning at 9 AM, station master Li Jiasheng accompanied Bai to inspect railway administration, intending to return to Shanghai on the same train at 2:38 PM in the afternoon. At 10:20 AM, the No. 3 Government Car was pushed onto the turntable by mechanics in order to turn it around and attach it to the passenger train heading to Shanghai. The car only rotated halfway on the turntable. Unexpectedly, the brakes on the car were not properly applied, and the wheel still moved forward. Although the mechanics tried to stop it, it was too late, and the car derailed. Fortunately, it was stopped by the old pump house at that location, preventing the entire car from derailing. Later, station master Li ordered workers to lift the car, and the damage was minor. Bai then took a passenger train to inspect stations such as Shitangwan.

Three Changzhou School Inspectors Arrive in Changzhou for Inspection

The exchange of school inspectors among counties in Jiangsu Province has recently been implemented separately. The three inspectors have separately decided on inspection areas and departed on the 8th. Yang Binru is responsible for the first and second school districts, Huang Yue is responsible for the third and fourth school districts, and Peng Shifang is responsible for the first and sixth school districts. The six schools inspected by Huang Yue are: Miduqiao, Tianning, the attached elementary school of the Normal School for Women, Chongzhen, Huacheng, and Zhichao. The seven schools inspected by Peng Shifang are: Juqian Street, Renfan, Dongmen, Shenyuan, Yinjiaqiao, Dongjiao Citizen, Xi Zhi, etc.

Gong Atang of Jiading Commits Suicide by Swallowing Opium

Gong Atang of Mengjin Township, because he relied on violence to bully people and committed all kinds of evil deeds, was known as "Ye Tang" (Wild Tang). In October of the year before last, Wang He, Gao Jiren, and others who had accumulated resentment against him, beat him severely and gouged out his eyes. His stepfather Ji Shun sued the county government. After investigation, Wang He was arrested and sentenced to fifteen years in prison. After becoming blind, Ye Tang could no longer carry out his extortion and his income decreased sharply. He felt great pain and asked someone to buy opium to commit suicide, but the person gave him a placebo and failed. On the 2nd of this month, he lost money gambling in the Mengjiangtang teahouse and became even more depressed. He hired a child to help him to Liuhe, bought six jiao worth of opium, and swallowed it all on the way home. After going to bed, he died from poisoning. It was not until the next morning when his mother called him to get up that she knew he had committed suicide. His mother believed that Ye Tang's death was caused by Gao Jiren and others gouging out his eyes, so she went to Gao's house to cry bitterly for days, causing trouble in various ways. His stepfather Ji Shun again sued the county government, asking for an investigation. The county government sent personnel to investigate and confirmed that he had committed suicide by swallowing opium. After five days, his body was finally claimed on the 8th and taken home for burial.

Major Fire in Yigou Town, Gaoyou

The home of Wang Gui in Henan, Yigou Town, District 3, under the jurisdiction of the county, caught fire accidentally this morning (the 7th) at 9 AM due to carelessness while preparing breakfast. At that time, a strong wind was blowing, and the fire quickly spread to the surrounding houses. Although fire brigades from various places arrived to help, the wind fueled the fire and it was difficult to extinguish. As a result, fifteen houses, including Wang Baohui's house, Yongtaiheng, Yang Hengtai's general merchandise store, and Dong's silversmith shop, were burned down, causing significant losses.

Commemoration of the 9th Anniversary of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Death on the 10th of This Month

The City Party Headquarters is Actively Preparing

Notifying All Sectors to Send Representatives to Participate

Party and Government Discuss Afforestation Movement Yesterday

The 12th of this month is the 9th anniversary of the death of Dr. Sun Yat-sen, the Father of the Nation, as well as this year's Arbor Day. The City Party Headquarters is actively preparing for commemorative events in accordance with the procedures prescribed by the Central Government. The Executive Committee has decided that at 9:00 AM on the morning of the 12th, a memorial meeting for representatives from all sectors will be convened at the Xiaoximen Youth Propaganda Group. Each of the seven organizations, including the headquarters, will nominate one representative to form the presidium. Committee member Huang Zaoxiong was nominated as chairman of the meeting. A letter has been sent to the Municipal Government and other organizations, requesting them to each nominate one representative to serve as chairman and attend on time. Notices have been posted to inform all organizations, groups, schools, and party branches to send representatives with letters of introduction to participate. The details are as follows:

Commemorative Measures

Commemoration: (1) Convene a memorial meeting for representatives from all sectors of Shanghai to commemorate the 9th anniversary of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's death. (2) Date: March 12, 9:00 AM. (3) Venue: Xiaoximen Youth Propaganda Group. (4) Presidium: Consists of one representative each from the City Party Headquarters, the Municipal Government, the Headquarters, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the General Labor Union, the Municipal Farmers' Association, and the Municipal Education Association. Notice: It is hereby announced that March 12th is the 9th anniversary of the death of Dr. Sun Yat-sen, the Father of the Nation. This is of utmost importance, therefore, this notice is hereby given.

Party and Government Meeting

Tong Muge of the City Party Headquarters, Li Dachao of the Municipal Government, Wu Huanru of the Social Affairs Bureau, and Wang Keyong of the Education Bureau attended.
